    <script type="text/javascript" language="javascript">
        $("document").ready(function () {

            $('#btnSaveNewsletter').click(function () {

                if (!validateFormExtended('#nl-form-1', '#newsletterError', false, false))
                    return false;

                $('#newsletterError').hide()
                $.ajax({
                    type: "POST",
                    contentType: "application/json; charset=utf-8",
                    url: "/LocalServices/1.0/Account.svc/NewsletterUserSave",
                    dataType: "json",
                    cache: false,
                    data: '{"Email": "' + $('#newsletterEmail').val() + '","LanguageId": "' + "de" + '","FirstName": "","LastName": ""}',

                    timeout: 50000,
                    success: function (data) {
                        if (data != null && !data.d.Status.Error) {
                            $('#newsletterEmail').hide();
                            $('#btnSaveNewsletter').hide();
                            $('#newsletterSuccesse').html("Sie haben sich erfolgreich für den Newsletter angemeldet.");
                            $('#newsletterSuccesse').fadeIn(1000);
                        }
                        else {
                            $('#newsletterError').html("Leider ist ein Fehler aufgetreten. Bitte versuchen Sie es nochmals.");
                            $('#newsletterError').fadeIn();
                        }
                    },
                    error: function (xhr) {
                        alert(xhr.responseText);
                        if (xhr.responseText)
                            $('#newsletterError').html(xhr.responseText);
                        $('#newsletterError').fadeIn()
                        return;

                    }
                });
            });

        });

    </script>

        <script type="text/javascript" language="javascript">
        var valid=true;
        $("document").ready(function () {
            var languageID = "de";
            $("#mainSearchTextField,#mainSearchTextFieldM").autocomplete({
                source: function (request, response) {
                    $.ajax({
                        type: "POST",
                        contentType: "application/json; charset=utf-8",
                        url: "/LocalServices/1.0/Search.svc/AutoCompleteSearchQuery",
                        dataType: "json",
                        data: '{"searchString":"' + request.term.replace(/"/g, "\\\"") + '","languageId":"de"}',
                        success: function (obj) {
                            response($.map(obj.d.autoCompleteResult.SuggestedProducts, function (item) {
                                return {
                                    label: item.ProductName, //Suggestions
                                    value: item.ProductName, //InputField
                                    productID: item.ProductId,
                                    notificationID: item.NotificationId
                                }
                            }));
                        },
                        error: function (xhr) {
                            return;
                        }
                    });
                },
                minLength: 2,
                delay: 1000,
                select: function (event, ui) {valid=false;
                    $.ajax({
                        type: "POST",
                        contentType: "application/json; charset=utf-8",
                        url: "/LocalServices/1.0/Search.svc/AutoCompleteNotify",
                        dataType: "json",
                        data: '{"notificationID":"' + ui.item.notificationID + '"}',
                        success: function (obj) {
                        },
                        error: function (xhr) {
                            if (xhr.responseText) {
                                $("body").html(xhr.responseText);
                            }
                            return;
                        },
                        complete: function () {
                            $.ajax({
                                type: "GET",
                                contentType: "application/json; charset=utf-8",
                                url: "/LocalServices/1.0/Product.svc/ProductSEOGet?ProductId=" + ui.item.productID + "&LanguageId=" + languageID,
                                dataType: "json",
                                data: {},
                                success: function (obj) {
                                    if (obj.d.ProductSEO == null || obj.d.ProductSEO.length < 1)
                                        alert("product not found");
                                    else
                                        window.location = obj.d.ProductSEO.Url;
                                },
                                error: function (xhr) {
                                    if (xhr.responseText) {
                                        $("body").html(xhr.responseText);
                                    }
                                    return;
                                }
                            });
                        }
                    });
                },
                open: function () {
                    $(this).removeClass("ui-corner-all").removeClass("ui-corner-top");
                },
                close: function () {
                    $(this).removeClass("ui-corner-top").removeClass("ui-corner-all");
                }
            });

           
        });
    </script>

<script>
  $(document).ready(function(){
    var slider = $(".royalSlider").data('royalSlider');

    bannerDataLayerPush();

    slider.ev.on('rsAfterSlideChange', function (event) {
        bannerDataLayerPush();
    });
  });

  function bannerDataLayerPush(){
        var impressionObjectId = $(".royalSlider").data('royalSlider').currSlide.holder.find('.rsImpressionObjectId').val();
        var contentId = $(".royalSlider").data('royalSlider').currSlide.holder.find('.rsContentId').val();
        var contentName = $(".royalSlider").data('royalSlider').currSlide.holder.find('.rsContentName').val();
        var contentCreative = $(".royalSlider").data('royalSlider').currSlide.holder.find('.rsContentCreative').val();
        var contentPosition = $(".royalSlider").data('royalSlider').currSlide.holder.find('.rsContentPosition').val();

        if(window[impressionObjectId] != null){
         dataLayer.push(window[impressionObjectId]);
        }
        else {
         dataLayer.push({
            'event': 'EECpromotionImpression',
            'ecommerce': {
                'promoView': {
                    'promotions': [
                     {
                         'id': contentId,
                         'name': contentName,
                         'creative': contentCreative,
                         'position': contentPosition
                     }]
                }
            }
         });
        }
  }
</script>

$(document).ready(function () {
	var today = new Date();
	var weekday = today.getDay();
	var hour = today.getHours();
	
	// wenn der Wochentag zwischen Donnerstag (20 Uhr) und Samstag liegt --> Module
	if ((weekday === 2 && hour >= 20) || (weekday >= 3 && weekday <= 6)) {
		$("#outerTeaserModule").removeClass("hideTeaser").addClass("showTeaser");
	}
	// sonst --> Flyer Highlights
	else {
		$("#outerTeaserHighlights").removeClass("hideTeaser").addClass("showTeaser");
	}
});

<div class="display-none" id="bandrole-1"><strong>Was bedeutet Online-Preis?</strong><br />

Online-Angebote und Marktangebote können sich somit unterscheiden. Im Markt gelten Mitnahmepreise der im Markt verfügbaren Artikel und regional verhandelte Angebote zu den Konditionen vor Ort.</div>
